| 1:26:23| 11A is a resolution honoring the life and memory of the Honorable Pamela L. Reeves,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5183)|
| 1:26:29| Chief Judge of the U.S. District Court for the Eastern District of Tennessee,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5189)|
| 1:26:34| and expressing sincere condolences to her loved ones upon the occasion of her passing.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5194)|
| 1:26:40| Move to approve.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5200)|
| 1:26:41| Second.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5201)|
| 1:26:42| A motion made to approve by Vice Mayor McKenzie, seconded by Councilmember Parker, Testerman.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5202)|
| 1:26:49| Testerman.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5209)|
| 1:26:51| Councilmembers, this item and the next one are to commemorate and honor two very important women| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5211)|
| 1:26:59| in our community, and very respected women. And I would like to read into the record before you vote| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5219)|
| 1:27:07| the text of the resolution, because I think it's a beautiful tribute to someone who's very important| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5227)|
| 1:27:13| in my life, and I feel very influential to members of Council and to our city.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5233)|
| 1:27:19| So with your forbearance, I'm going to read the text of the resolution.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5239)|
| 1:27:23| Whereas the Honorable Pamela L. Reeves, Chief Judge of the United States District Court for| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5243)|
| 1:27:27| the Eastern District of Tennessee, passed away September 10, 2020, after a two-year| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5247)|
| 1:27:32| battle with cancer. And whereas Judge Reeves was born July 21, 1954, in Marion, Virginia,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5252)|
| 1:27:39| the eldest of five daughters to Fred and Betty Reeves, and lived in the mountains of| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5259)|
| 1:27:44| Grayson County, Virginia, in a four-room house with no running water. And whereas in 1970,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5264)|
| 1:27:51| to the great fortune of our community, Judge Reeves enrolled in classes at the University| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5271)|
| 1:27:55| of Tennessee, whereas the first in her family to attend college, she served as a torchbearer,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5275)|
| 1:28:02| graduated Phi Beta Kappa, and later earned her law degree. And whereas Judge Reeves demonstrated| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5282)|
| 1:28:08| her leadership and passion early, when during law school, she circulated petitions to save| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5288)|
| 1:28:14| the endangered snail darter, and assisted her professors in preparing arguments before the| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5294)|
| 1:28:18| United States Supreme Court, wherein to this day, and through the diligent work of Judge Reeves,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5298)|
| 1:28:24| the snail darter is a federally protected species of fish. And whereas Judge Reeves was a pioneer| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5304)|
| 1:28:30| and trailblazer for women, as a leading voice of the profession across the state early in her| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5310)|
| 1:28:35| career, when there were very few female lawyers in visible leadership roles in the legal community,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5315)|
| 1:28:40| notably in 1998, when she was elected as the first female president of the Tennessee Bar| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5320)|
| 1:28:46| Association, in 2014, when she was confirmed as the first female federal court judge of the| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5326)|
| 1:28:52| Eastern District of Tennessee, and in 2019, when she was appointed as the first female judge of| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5332)|
| 1:28:58| the Eastern District, first female chief judge of the Eastern District of Tennessee.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5338)|
| 1:29:04| And whereas Judge Reeves was not only a trailblazer for women, but for generations of lawyers across| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5344)|
| 1:29:10| the state of Tennessee and around the country, through her talent for identifying and amplifying| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5350)|
| 1:29:14| the best in lawyers, her willingness to assist and mentor young lawyers in their practice,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5354)|
| 1:29:19| and her persistence in pushing fellow lawyers to dedicate time and energy to the advancement of the| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5359)|
| 1:29:24| profession and the improvement of the legal community. And whereas despite her national| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5364)|
| 1:29:29| reputation as a lawyer and judge of the highest order, Judge Reeves never abandoned her true| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5369)|
| 1:29:34| Southern roots, including her passion for perfecting the art of making sausage gravy,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5374)|
| 1:29:39| her devotion to gardening, her love of the mountains, and her infatuation with Kris Kristofferson.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5379)|
| 1:29:46| And whereas Judge Reeves was the devoted wife of our own Charles W. Swanson, city law director,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5386)|
| 1:29:53| and loving mother of Reedy Swanson and Amanda Swanson, two accomplished attorneys in their| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5393)|
| 1:29:58| own right, and the quality of Judge Reeves as a person is evident in her remarkable family,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5398)|
| 1:30:02| for which this council holds the highest regard. And whereas while it is not possible to fully| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5402)|
| 1:30:07| catalog the achievements of Judge Reeves or the impact her life had upon the many people she knew,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5407)|
| 1:30:13| two awards she received in the final months of her life demonstrate the extraordinary nature| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5413)|
| 1:30:18| of this woman. The inaugural Tennessee Bar Association Professionalism Award given to a| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5418)|
| 1:30:23| lawyer or judge whose life and practice display sterling character and unquestioned integrity,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5423)|
| 1:30:30| coupled with ongoing dedication to the highest standards of the rule of law and the highest| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5430)|
| 1:30:34| standards of the legal profession in Tennessee, and the highest honor to be bestowed upon alumni| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5434)|
| 1:30:39| of the University of Tennessee, the Distinguished Alumna Award for Extraordinary Distinction and| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5439)|
| 1:30:44| Success. And whereas her efforts to better lawyers in the practice of law will be felt by| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5444)|
| 1:30:48| generations of lawyers, Knoxvillians, and Tennesseans, as countless individuals have| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5448)|
| 1:30:53| recently expressed the tremendous and positive impact she had upon them personally and professionally,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5453)|

| 1:38:32| Whereas Mary B. DeSelme passed away on Sunday, September 6, 2020, at the age of 95 years.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5912)|
| 1:38:39| And whereas Ms. DeSelme was born Mary Elizabeth Hersey, grew up in Columbus, Ohio,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5919)|
| 1:38:44| and went to nursing school at Ohio State University. And whereas Ms. DeSelme and her| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5924)|
| 1:38:48| husband Hal moved to Knoxville in 1956. And whereas Ms. DeSelme was a nurse for 10 years| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5928)|
| 1:38:55| and then was religious education director for 12 years at Tennessee Valley Unitarian| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5935)|
| 1:38:59| Universalist Church. And whereas in 1976, Ms. DeSelme was elected to the Knox County Court,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5939)|
| 1:39:05| becoming one of the first women in modern history to serve on the body that became the Knox County| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5945)|
| 1:39:10| Commission in 1980. And whereas during her years in office, Ms. DeSelme served on the education| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5950)|
| 1:39:15| committee, including as chair and was among those who helped lead Knox County to achieve a single| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5955)|
| 1:39:20| school system in 1987. And whereas Ms. DeSelme continued to serve on the Knox County Commission| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5960)|
| 1:39:26| until 1998, when she decided not to seek re-election out of respect for the passage of| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5966)|
| 1:39:31| term limits in 1994 by Knox County voters. The term limits would not actually be enforced until| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5971)|
| 1:39:37| a Tennessee Supreme Court decision in 2007. And whereas Ms. DeSelme was mentored in politics and| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5977)|
| 1:39:43| local government by Mayor Victor Ashe, and subsequently she mentored Mayors Madeline| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5983)|
| 1:39:48| O'Hara and India Kincaid in their early political careers as county commissioner and school board| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5988)|
| 1:39:53| member, respectively. And whereas Ms. DeSelme was honored in 1995 with the Religious Service Award| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5993)|
| 1:39:59| from the National Conference, formerly the National Conference of Christians and Jews,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=5999)|
| 1:40:03| which described Ms. DeSelme as believing that, quote, one's purpose in life is to work to make| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=6003)|
| 1:40:10| one's community serve the needs of its people. And whereas in 2000, the West Knoxville branch| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=6010)|
| 1:40:15| of the Knox County Public Library System was named the B. DeSelme Building in honor of Ms. DeSelme.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=6015)|
| 1:40:20| And whereas Ms. DeSelme was honored in 2014 by the YWCA Knoxville during its annual Tribute to| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=6020)|
| 1:40:26| Women as one of 30 women who impacted the community in the previous 30 years. And whereas Ms. DeSelme| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=6026)|
| 1:40:32| was a member of Leadership Knoxville Class of 1990, the Knoxville-Knox County Community Action| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=6032)|
| 1:40:37| Committee's Community Leadership Class of 1995, the Domestic Violence Task Force, the Community| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=6037)|
| 1:40:42| Alternatives to Prison Board, the Metropolitan Planning Commission, the Historic Zoning Commission,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=6042)|
| 1:40:47| the American Cancer Society Public Issues Committee, and she chaired the Public Affairs| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=6047)|
| 1:40:52| Committee of the National Conference. And whereas Ms. DeSelme will be deeply missed| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=6052)|

| 1:59:13| Chad West, City Public Service Director.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7153)|
| 1:59:16| Yeah, this is kind of a confusing project if you haven't seen it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7156)|
| 1:59:20| We actually had this scheduled to be done last year.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7160)|
| 1:59:24| Only because of the compactor and the pits and the way they are designed,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7164)|
| 1:59:29| they are considered a confined space.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7169)|
| 1:59:31| So the contractor that we had then wasn't perfectly comfortable, so we have rebid it now.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7171)|
| 1:59:36| And this is for Ziggurat to do this work.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7176)|
| 1:59:39| So what it is is where you push the waste into the compactors over time.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7179)|
| 1:59:45| The waste at the bottom of these compactors basically,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7185)|
| 1:59:48| just like anything else, starts to deteriorate and wear out.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7188)|
| 1:59:51| So there are some holes in the bottom of the pit area where waste can gather.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7191)|
| 1:59:57| And of course, where waste gathers, you have more availability for rodents to be.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7197)|
| 2:00:02| And obviously, it's hard to get all the waste out when you have these holes.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7202)|
| 2:00:06| So in addition to the holes in the bottom of the pits,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7206)|
| 2:00:08| there's also an old push paddle that has not been used in 15 years.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7208)|
| 2:00:12| It used to be, that's basically a big arm| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7212)|
| 2:00:14| that used to come and push the garbage into the pit areas.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7214)|
| 2:00:18| Really, it's not the most efficient because garbage inevitably goes outside of the reach| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7218)|
| 2:00:23| of the push paddle and you have to use a front end loader to push the garbage in anyway.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7223)|
| 2:00:28| So we have been using that method for the last 15 years, longer than I've been here,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7228)|
| 2:00:33| in order to push the waste into that pit.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7233)|
| 2:00:36| So it's a little confusing unless you've seen it,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-200922_202102?start=7236)|
